(assert (forall ((?x TermBool) (?y TermBool)) (= (= (boolIff ?x ?y) boolTrue) (= (= ?x boolTrue) (= ?y boolTrue)))))
(assert (forall ((?x TermBool) (?y TermBool)) (= (= (boolImplies ?x ?y) boolTrue) (=> (= ?x boolTrue) (= ?y boolTrue)))))
(assert (forall ((?x TermBool) (?y TermBool)) (= (= (boolAnd ?x ?y) boolTrue) (and (= ?x boolTrue) (= ?y boolTrue)))))
(assert (forall ((?x TermBool) (?y TermBool)) (= (= (boolOr ?x ?y) boolTrue) (or (= ?x boolTrue) (= ?y boolTrue)))))
(assert (forall ((?x TermBool)) (! (= (= (boolNot ?x) boolTrue) (not (= ?x boolTrue))) :pattern ((boolNot ?x)) )))
(assert (forall ((?x boogieU) (?y boogieU)) (= (= (UEqual ?x ?y) boolTrue) (= ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x boogieT) (?y boogieT)) (= (= (TEqual ?x ?y) boolTrue) (= ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x Int) (?y Int)) (= (= (IntEqual ?x ?y) boolTrue) (= ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x Int) (?y Int)) (= (= (intLess ?x ?y) boolTrue) (< ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x Int) (?y Int)) (= (= (intAtMost ?x ?y) boolTrue) (<= ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x Int) (?y Int)) (= (= (intAtLeast ?x ?y) boolTrue) (>= ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x Int) (?y Int)) (= (= (intGreater ?x ?y) boolTrue) (> ?x ?y))))
(assert (distinct boolFalse boolTrue))
(assert (forall ((?x boogieU) (?y boogieU)) (= (= (TermUOrdering2 ?x ?y) boolTrue) (UOrdering2 ?x ?y))))
(assert (forall ((?x boogieT) (?y boogieU) (?z boogieU)) (= (= (TermUOrdering3 ?x ?y ?z) boolTrue) (UOrdering3 ?x ?y ?z))))
